</ul>

    <div id="wiki-content" class="mt-4">
      <div data-view-component="true" class="Layout Layout--flowRow-until-md Layout--sidebarPosition-end Layout--sidebarPosition-flowRow-end">
  <div data-view-component="true" class="Layout-main">          <div id="wiki-body" class="gollum-markdown-content">
              <div class="markdown-body">
                <p>âœ¨ Read the getting started <a href="Home#getting-started-">here</a> <br>
Roblox properties are merged with the configuration of an element.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h1 class="heading-element">Sliders</h1><a id="user-content-sliders" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Sliders" href="#sliders"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewbox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">Properties</h3><a id="user-content-properties" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Properties" href="#properties"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewbox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul>
<li><code>Label = string</code></li>
<li>
<code>Format = "%.d"</code> - <a href="https://web.archive.org/web/20250209112416/https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/libraries/string#format" rel="nofollow">:format Documentation</a> (Value, MaxValue)</li>
<li><code>Value = 0</code></li>
<li><code>MinValue = int</code></li>
<li><code>MaxValue = int</code></li>
<li><code>ReadOnly = false</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">Methods</h3><a id="user-content-methods" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Methods" href="#methods"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewbox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul>
<li><code>:SetValue(Value: int)</code></li>
<li><code>:FireCallback(...)</code></li>
<li><code>:SetCallback(Callback: function)</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">Example</h3><a id="user-content-example" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Example" href="#example"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewbox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-lua notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="Tab:Slider({
	Label = &quot;Slider&quot;,
	Format = &quot;%.d/%s&quot;, 
	Value = 5,
	MinValue = 1,
	MaxValue = 32,

	Callback = function(self, Value)
		print(self.Name, Value)
	end,
})"><pre><span class="pl-en">Tab</span>:<span class="pl-c1">Slider</span>({
	<span class="pl-smi">Label</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Slider<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
	<span class="pl-smi">Format</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>%.d/%s<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, 
	<span class="pl-smi">Value</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span>,
	<span class="pl-smi">MinValue</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>,
	<span class="pl-smi">MaxValue</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">32</span>,

	<span class="pl-en">Callback</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">self</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Value</span>)
		<span class="pl-c1">print</span>(<span class="pl-c1">self</span>.<span class="pl-e">Name</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Value</span>)
	<span class="pl-k">end</span>,
})</pre></div>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-lua notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="local ProgressBar = Tab:ProgressBar({
	Label = &quot;Loading...&quot;,
	Percentage = 80
})


spawn(function()
	local Percentage = 0
	while wait(.02) do
		Percentage += 1
		ProgressBar:SetPercentage(Percentage % 100)
	end
end)"><pre><span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">ProgressBar</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-en">Tab</span>:<span class="pl-c1">ProgressBar</span>({
	<span class="pl-smi">Label</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Loading...<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
	<span class="pl-smi">Percentage</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">80</span>
})


<span class="pl-c1">spawn</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>()
	<span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">Percentage</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>
	<span class="pl-k">while</span> <span class="pl-c1">wait</span>(<span class="pl-c1">.02</span>) <span class="pl-k">do</span>
		<span class="pl-smi">Percentage</span> <span class="pl-k">+=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>
		<span class="pl-en">ProgressBar</span>:<span class="pl-c1">SetPercentage</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Percentage</span> <span class="pl-k">%</span> <span class="pl-c1">100</span>)

<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">Methods</h3><a id="user-content-methods-4" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Methods" href="#methods-4"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewbox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-lua notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="local RunService = game:GetService(&quot;RunService&quot;)
local Viewport = Tab:Viewport({
	Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 200),
	Clone = true, --// Otherwise will parent
	Model = Rig,
	Border = false
})

local NewRig = Viewport:SetModel(Rig, CFrame.new(0, -2.5, -5))

--// Spin rig
RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function(deltaTime)
	local YRotation = 30 * deltaTime
	local cFrame = NewRig:GetPivot() * CFrame.Angles(0,math.rad(YRotation),0)
	NewRig:PivotTo(cFrame)
end)"><pre><span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">RunService</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-en">game</span>:<span class="pl-c1">GetService</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>RunService<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)

<div class="highlight highlight-source-lua notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="local Console = Tab:Console({
	Text = &quot;Console example&quot;,
	ReadOnly = true,
	Border = false,
	Fill = true,
	RichText = true,
	Enabled = true, 
	AutoScroll = true,
	MaxLines = 50
})

Tab:Button({ --// Toggle to enable the console
	Text = &quot;Pause&quot;,
	Callback = function(self)
		local Paused = shared.Pause
		Paused = not (Paused or false)
		shared.Pause = Paused
		
		self.Text = Paused and &quot;Paused&quot; or &quot;Pause&quot;
		Console.Enabled = not Paused
	end,
})

spawn(function()
	while wait() do
		Console:AppendText( --// Passed parameters will be concatenated 
			`<font color=&quot;rgb(240, 40, 10)&quot;>[Random Math]</font>`, 
			math.random()
		)
	end
end)"><pre><span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">Console</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-en">Tab</span>:<span class="pl-c1">Console</span>({
	<span class="pl-smi">Text</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Console example<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
	<span class="pl-smi">ReadOnly</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>,
	<span class="pl-smi">Border</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">false</span>,
	<span class="pl-smi">Fill</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>,
	<span class="pl-smi">RichText</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>,
	<span class="pl-smi">Enabled</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>, 
	<span class="pl-smi">AutoScroll</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>,
	<span class="pl-smi">MaxLines</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">50</span>
})

<span class="pl-en">Tab</span>:<span class="pl-c1">Button</span>({ <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span>// Toggle to enable the console</span>
	<span class="pl-smi">Text</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
	<span class="pl-en">Callback</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">self</span>)
		<span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">Paused</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">shared</span>.<span class="pl-e">Pause</span>
		<span class="pl-smi">Paused</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">not</span> (<span class="pl-smi">Paused</span> <span class="pl-k">or</span> <span class="pl-c1">false</span>)
		<span class="pl-smi">shared</span>.<span class="pl-e">Pause</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">Paused</span>
		
		<span class="pl-c1">self</span>.<span class="pl-e">Text</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">Paused</span> <span class="pl-k">and</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Paused<span class="pl-pds">" </span></span><span class="pl-k">or</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
		<span class="pl-smi">Console</span>.<span class="pl-e">Enabled</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">not</span> <span class="pl-smi">Paused</span>
	<span class="pl-k">end</span>,
})

<span class="pl-c1">spawn</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>()
	<span class="pl-k">while</span> <span class="pl-c1">wait</span>() <span class="pl-k">do</span>
		<span class="pl-en">Console</span>:<span class="pl-c1">AppendText</span>( <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span>// Passed parameters will be concatenated </span>
			<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>&lt;font color="rgb(240, 40, 10)"&gt;[Random Math]&lt;/font&gt;<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>, 
			<span class="pl-c1">math.random</span>()
		)
	<span class="pl-k">end</span>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-lua notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="local Table = Tab:Table({
	RowBackground = true,
	Border = true,
	RowsFill = false,
	Size = UDim2.fromScale(1, 0)
})

coroutine.wrap(function()
	local Rows = 10
	local random = Random.new()
	while wait(1) do
		Table:ClearRows()
		
		for i = 1,Rows do
			local Row = Table:CreateRow()

			local Columns = random:NextInteger(1, 8)
			for x = 1, Columns do
				local Column = Row:CreateColumn()
				Column:Label({
					Text = `#{x}`
				})
			end
		end
	end
end)()"><pre><span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">Table</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-en">Tab</span>:<span class="pl-c1">Table</span>({
	<span class="pl-smi">RowBackground</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>,
	<span class="pl-smi">Border</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>,
	<span class="pl-smi">RowsFill</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">false</span>,
	<span class="pl-smi">Size</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">UDim2</span>.<span class="pl-c1">fromScale</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>)
})

<span class="pl-c1">coroutine.wrap</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>()
	<span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">Rows</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">10</span>
	<span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">random</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">Random</span>.<span class="pl-c1">new</span>()
	<span class="pl-k">while</span> <span class="pl-c1">wait</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>) <span class="pl-k">do</span>
		<span class="pl-en">Table</span>:<span class="pl-c1">ClearRows</span>()
		
		<span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-smi">i</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-smi">Rows</span> <span class="pl-k">do</span>
			<span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">Row</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-en">Table</span>:<span class="pl-c1">CreateRow</span>()

			<span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">Columns</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-en">random</span>:<span class="pl-c1">NextInteger</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>, <span class="pl-c1">8</span>)
			<span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-smi">x</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Columns</span> <span class="pl-k">do</span>
				<span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">Column</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-en">Row</span>:<span class="pl-c1">CreateColumn</span>()
				<span class="pl-en">Column</span>:<span class="pl-c1">Label</span>({
					<span class="pl-smi">Text</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>#{x}<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>
				})
			<span class="pl-k">end</span>
		<span class="pl-k">end</span>
	<span class="pl-k">end</span>
<span class="pl-k">end</span>)()</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h1 class="heading-element">Combos/Dropdowns</h1><a id="user-content-combosdropdowns" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Combos/Dropdowns" href="#combosdropdowns"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewbox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">Properties</h3><a id="user-content-properties-12" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Properties" href="#properties-12"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewbox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul>
<li><code>Placeholder = string</code></li>
<li><code>Callback = function</code></li>
<li><code>Items = Dict/Array</code></li>
<li><code>NoAnimation = false</code></li>
<li>
<code>Value = string</code> (Previously .Selected)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">Methods</h3><a id="user-content-methods-12" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Methods" href="#methods-12"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewbox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul>
<li><code>:SetOpen(Open: boolean)</code></li>
<li><code>:SetValue(Item: string)</code></li>
<li><code>:GetValue()</code></li>
<li><code>:FireCallback(...)</code></li>
<li><code>:SetCallback(Callback: function)</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">Example</h3><a id="user-content-example-15" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Example" href="#example-15"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewbox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-lua notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="Tab:Combo({
	Selected = &quot;Car&quot;, --// Cancels Placeholder 
	Label = &quot;Vehicle&quot;,
	Items = {
		&quot;Car&quot;,
		&quot;Bus&quot;,
		&quot;Train&quot;,
		&quot;Plane&quot;,
		&quot;Boat&quot;
	},
	Callback = function(self, Value)
		print(&quot;Selected:&quot;, Value)
	end,
})

Tab:Combo({
	Placeholder = &quot;Select object&quot;,
	Label = &quot;Food&quot;,
	Items = {
		[&quot;Apple&quot;] = &quot;Good&quot;,
		[&quot;Banana&quot;] = &quot;Bad&quot;,
		[&quot;Mango&quot;] = &quot;Okay&quot;
	},
	Callback = function(self, Value)
		print(&quot;Selected:&quot;, Value, &quot;Value:&quot;, self.Items[Value])
	end,
})"><pre><span class="pl-en">Tab</span>:<span class="pl-c1">Combo</span>({
	<span class="pl-smi">Selected</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Car<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span>// Cancels Placeholder </span>
	<span class="pl-smi">Label</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Vehicle<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
	<span class="pl-smi">Items</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> {
		<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Car<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
		<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Bus<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
		<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Train<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,

	},
	<span class="pl-en">Callback</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">self</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Value</span>)
		<span class="pl-c1">print</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Selected:<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">Value</span>)
	<span class="pl-k">end</span>,
})

<span class="pl-en">Tab</span>:<span class="pl-c1">Combo</span>({
	<span class="pl-smi">Placeholder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Select object<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,

<div class="markdown-heading"><h1 class="heading-element">Modals</h1><a id="user-content-modals" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Modals" href="#modals"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewbox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">Properties &amp; Methods</h3><a id="user-content-properties--methods" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Properties &amp; Methods" href="#properties--methods"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewbox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">Example</h3><a id="user-content-example-16" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Example" href="#example-16"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewbox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-lua notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="local ModalWindow = ImGui:CreateModal({ --// Returns a Tab class
	Title = &quot;Modal Example&quot;,
	AutoSize = &quot;Y&quot;
})

ModalWindow:Label({
	Text = &quot;Hello, this is a modal.&quot;
})
ModalWindow:Separator()

ModalWindow:Button({
	Text = &quot;Okay&quot;,
	Callback = function()
		ModalWindow:Close()
	end,
})"><pre><span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">ModalWindow</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-en">ImGui</span>:<span class="pl-c1">CreateModal</span>({ <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span>// Returns a Tab class</span>

	<span class="pl-smi">AutoSize</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Y<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-en">ModalWindow</span>:<span class="pl-c1">Label</span>({
